Windows update will not run (Red Shield) Error message: - Microsoft Community

tim998765 say:

Windows update will not run (Red Shield) Error message: Windows Update can not currently check for updates, because the service is not running.

I'm running Vista x64 Business SP2.  (Version 6.0 (Build 6002: Service Pack2)).

The PC has a dual i7-x920 and 12G of RAM.

I last updated my PC on 26 JUN 2012 and haven't been able to update since.  There were 70 various updates, primarily for Visual C++, Visual Studio 2010 pro, .NET Framework 4, and MS Office (w/ Office 2007 SP3).

I have a Red Shield and when I click on the Update button I get the following POP UP window:

"Windows Update can not currently check for updates, because the service is not running.  You may need to restart your computer."

I've logged in as Administrator and as my normal user (where all the updates have run before).

I see that the Windows Update Service is not running, nor is it present. 

wuauserv.dll is in the Windows/system32 directory with a size of 6,656 bytes with a date of 21 SEP 2012.

This is a "Genuine MS product", it has been activated, and has the MS logo on the "Basic System page" (Control Panel\System).

Thank you for your support

 

Tim

winston m say:

Hi Tim998765,

 

 

Thank you for posting the question. I will surely help you to find a resolution regarding the Windows update issue.

 

1.       Which is the antivirus program installed on the computer?

2.       Are you aware of making any changes to the computer prior to the issue?

3.       What is the size of the hard disk present on the computer? Is it more than 500GB?

 

Method 1:


You may run the fixit. Refer the following link.

Fix the problem with Microsoft Windows Update that is not working
http://support.microsoft.com/mats/windows_update/

 

 

Method 2: Perform the steps provided in the article

Error: Windows Update Cannot Check For Updates, Because the Service Is Not Running

 

 

Run Microsoft Fixit tool mentioned in the article: http://support.microsoft.com/kb/2730071

Once you perform these steps, try to install Windows Update and check if it helps.

 

 

 

 

Method 3: Rename the SoftwareDistribution folder

Rename the Windows Update temporary SoftwareDistribution folder. To do this, follow these steps:

 

 

1.            Open an administrative Command Prompt window.

2.            Run the following commands, and press Enter after each command:

Net stop wuauserv

cd %systemroot%

Ren SoftwareDistribution SoftwareDistribution.old

Net start wuauserv

4.       Try to install updates again.

 

Refer:

 

Unable to install updates in Windows Vista, Windows 7, Windows Server 2008 and Windows Server 2008 R2

http://support.microsoft.com/kb/2509997

Note: This section, method, or task contains steps that tell you how to modify the registry. However, serious problems might occur if you modify the registry incorrectly. Therefore, make sure that you follow these steps carefully. For added protection, back up the registry before you modify it. Then, you can restore the registry if a problem occurs. For more information about how to back up and restore the registry, click the following article number to view the article in the Microsoft Knowledge Base. How to back up and restore the registry in Windows:

http://windows.microsoft.com/en-US/windows7/Back-up-the-registry

 

 

Hope this information helps. Please reply back with the status so that we could help you further.

    Question about regions... - Microsoft Community

    arcticdeer54477 say:

    Question about regions...

    Hi,

    I have a question. Since people got banned for downloading "free" games from Oman there are several rumours about buying games from foreign marketplaces. Every player above 500k GS (and probably a lot below) has done that to get content from Japan, Germany and some other countries.

    So my questions are:

    1. Am I allowed to buy and download content from foreign countries? People got banned for "Utilizing fraudulent methods in order to obtain region-specific marketplace content or circumvent regional pricing" but even people like Microsoft's favourite gamer (italian) S*******83 obviously did that. Or is it only illegal to get free games that are not supposed to be free? They ban people for this but you cannot find any information about this.

    2. When I move from country A to country B do I have to migrate my account to country B even though some content is not available in country B? Or can I create a new account with the current region that I can use my old account to download my purchased content which is not available in my new region.

    3. Some content has IP restrictions. same example...when I move from country A to country B am I allowed to use VPN services to download and use the content I have paid for? I do not mean buying new stuff. I am talking about content I have paid for in country A. For example I would like to download everything again when I buy a new console.

    Thank you

    midnightiecx say:

    Hello ArcticDeer54477,


    1. You are allowed to purchase content from a different country. But you'll also have to purchase a different Xbox since there are so many games that are region locked. Let's use Japan as an example. If you're console can only play NTSC, it will not play NTSC-J. Unless the games are Region-Free. (PAL, NTSC, NTSC-J)


    2. Migrating your account is only optional. If you move from country A to B and want all content from B to be added to your main XBL account, then you can migrate your account. If not, you can simply create a new account.


    3. From my understanding of things, VPN services are not allowed. You can keep your previous console, have all of that content from A on that console. And from B, you can have the content on there.

    silentpages say:

    The games that are free in those countries are free because of differences between the Xbox LIVE service.

    If a game is free in a other country it could be for promotion or anything else.

    If you start to download them and change your region, you get in trouble. 

    I don´t know why you are asking this.

    VPN is also a two sided blade. 

    Just because people do it and get away with it does not mean they won´t get in trouble one day. 

    If you want a honest answer on all your questions, do not do what you asked.

    Of course it´s different if you pay for the games.

    xbox_series_x|s_and_xbox_one,

    External Hard Drive Recognized As Media Only Will Not Reformat - Microsoft Community

    cincyred say:

    External Hard Drive Recognized As Media Only Will Not Reformat

    Purchased a Seagate Xbox One External HD, 2TB. Plugged it in and Xbox One will only recognize it as media player. How can I reformat it for games and apps? I have searched and it looks like a menu should appear at this stage:

    1. Scroll left from Home to open the guide.
    2. Select Settings.
    3. Select Allsettings.
    4. Select System.
    5. Select Storage.
    6. Select External Drive.

    No menu appears to reformat. Am I missing something?

    {parity} say:

    Try this.  I have had it work for some users.  Disconnect the external drive.  Then do a hard reset like this.  Please follow the directions exactly.  Hold the power button on the console for 10 seconds or until the power shuts down completely.  Unplug the power cord from the back of the console for 5 minutes.  Plug the power cord back in and restart the console.   Once it is back up and operational connect the external HDD and test for results.  Let  us know.  Good Luck!

    I have a Lifecam cinema how do you turn the auto focus off? - Microsoft Community

    tynecub say:

    I have a Lifecam cinema how do you turn the auto focus off?

    I downloaded the latest software for windows 7 64 bit which came on the CD when I purchased it last night.

    This does seem to be more upto date than what is available on the microsoft website.


    Looking on other sites most people are saying go into properties and settings.  I do not have this option on the Lifecam software, so can anyone help as I am finding the autofocus anoying although a very good picture.


    Cheers
    mc0121 say:

    I'm currently using version 3.21.263.0. Open the lifecam software, click the blue arrow button located on the right side of the window, click the little gear at the top, uncheck the truecolor box, and a properties button should appear. After you click it, go to the camera control tab, and uncheck the box that says auto, on the focus section.

    Hope this helps.

    Unire un profilo Offline con un profilo Xbox Live

    Unire il nome di un profilo Offline con quello di un profilo Xbox Live

    Se hai creato un profilo Offline sulla tua console e vuoi tenerlo, ed hai anche creato un profilo su Xbox.com, essenzialmente possiedi due profili distinti: uno sulla tua console ed uno in Xbox Live.

    Per poter utilizzare il tuo profilo Offline in Xbox Live con lo stesso Gamertag e con tutti i tuoi obiettivi (e relativo Gamerscore) intatti, devi sostituire il tuo profilo Xbox Live con quello Offline.

    I mezzi per far questo sono presenti sulla tua Xbox 360, bisogna solo saperli usare:

    NOTA

    Questa procedura non è applicabile a chiunque sia già membro di Xbox Live prima di utilizzare Xbox 360 per la prima volta. Questa guida è rivolta ad utenti Xbox 360 che hanno sbloccato obiettivi con un profilo Offline e che hanno creato un profilo su Xbox.com prima di partecipare ad Xbox Live. Se non sei interessato a mantenere i tuoi obiettivi ed il tuo punteggio giocatore, non c’è motivo di seguire questa procedura.

    In questo esempio, il Gamertag in entrambi i casi è TR1GG3R MAN. Cioè sia il profilo Offline che quello Xbox Live (creato su Xbox.com) si chiamano TR1GG3R MAN.

    • 1. Dalla Dashboard o dalla Guida Xbox scegli il profilo Offline e seleziona Modifica Profilo Giocatore.
    • 2. Seleziona Nome Profilo.
    • 3. Inserisci un nuovo Nome Profilo, per esempio TR1GG3R MAN01.
      (In alternativa potresti spostare il tuo profilo Offline su una Memory Unit Xbox 360 senza cambiarne il nome)
    • 4. Esci dalla Dashboard premendo X.
    • 5. Dalla blade Xbox Live seleziona Partecipa a Xbox Live e segui le indicazioni sullo schermo.
    • 6. Alla schermata Gamertag, inserisci il tuo Gamertag, TR1GG3R MAN.
    • 7. Quando ti appare il messaggio di Gamertag In Uso, seleziona Ripristina Gamertag e segui le indicazioni sullo schermo.
    • 8. Assicurati di avere i dati del tuo .NET Passport a portata di mano e di scegliere l’abbonamento gratuito Xbox Live Silver, in quanto, dopo questa procedura, probabilmente non utilizzerai questa sottoscrizione.
    • 9. Una volta recuperato il tuo profilo Xbox.com sulla tua console, ripeti i punti 1 e 2 sopraelencati per cambiare il nome di questo profilo in qualcosa di diverso da TR1GG3R MAN, per esempio TR1GG3R MAN02. (Da Modifica Profilo Giocatore, seleziona Gamertag) 

    NOTA

    Dovrai riscattare dei Microsoft Points per cambiare un Gamertag collegato ad un profilo Xbox Live. Se non hai Microsoft Points disponibili, ti verrà data l’opzione di acquistarli. Per maggiori informazioni, clicca qui.

    • 10. A questo punto avrai due profili, nessuno dei quali si chiama TR1GG3R MAN.
    • 11. TR1GG3R MAN è ora disponibile.
    • 12. Esci dalla Dashboard premendo X.
    • 13. Seleziona “Connetti”, poi seleziona il tuo profilo Offline, TR1GG3R MAN01.
    • 14. Prima che qualcuno ti prenda il Gamertag, ripeti i punti 1 e 2 per cambiare il nome del tuo profilo Offline (il quale è associato a tutti i tuoi giochi ed al tuo Gamerscore) da TR1GG3R MAN01 a TR1GG3R MAN. 
      (Se hai utilizzato una Memory Unit al punto 3, adesso è il momento di spostare il profilo Offline di nuovo sulla console)
    • 15. Ripeti il punto 5 per Partecipare ad Xbox Live utilizzando il tuo Gamertag originale, TR1GG3R MAN. Dovrai creare od utilizzare un .NET Passport alternativo, siccome TR1GG3R MAN02 rimarrà collegato al tuo .NET Passport originale.
    • 16. Adesso puoi cancellare il profilo TR1GG3R MAN02 dalla tua console.

     

    Fonte la vecchia pagina FAQ del vecchio forum, se hai dubbi o altre domande chiedi pure, Welcome su Xbox Live

    I just updated to windows 10, how do I get my favorites list of - Microsoft Community

    kjg50 say:

    I just updated to windows 10, how do I get my favorites list of bookmarks to display ?

    I just updated to windows 10, so how do I get my favorites bookmark list to display

    a. user say:

    Hi,

    Thank you for posting on Microsoft Community. I will certainly help you with this. I appreciate if you could answer few questions to narrow down the issue and to provide you better assistance.

    1. Where is favorite list of bookmarks stored on PC’s hard drive?
    2. Where exactly you want Favorite list to be displayed?
    3. Are the bookmarks saved for Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge?

    You can pin it under Library in Windows file explorer by following the below given steps:

    • Right click on desired folder that is to be displayed under library.
    • Click on show in Library and click on the folder under which it is to be displayed.

    Please post back with the results and the information asked, we will be glad to assist you further.

    Thank you.

    kjg50 say:

    As far as where is the list stored on my hard drive, ... I don't know. I had it stored in internet explorer, all I had to do to view it was click on the star on the task/tool bar, you know, the ... big yellow star ?
    That's where I would like to continue to click to view. Can you help ?

    jckhudg say:

    Your favorites for Edge are stored at:

    C:\Users\[user name]\AppData\Local\Packages\Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe\AC\MicrosoftEdge\User\Default\Favorites

    ... where [user name] is your login name.

    What I like to do is create a toolbar for favorites.  To do this, right-click on the taskbar, and choose toolbars -> new folder.  Navigate your way to the oddball folder above, click on "select folder" and you'll end up with a nice menu of your favorites on the right side of the taskbar.

    beerboy1953 say:

    At the right of the bar that has the URL on it , you will see 3 horizontal lines above each other next to a box with a pencil on it. Left click on the 3 lines. You will see your missing star!

    Click on it and your favorites will be shown. Also is a clickable import favorites word.

    Mine were there when I clicked the star. Good luck.

    ybnice say: Thanks very much JckHudg.

    kenthardin say: This did not help me.  I want the favorites that were in my internet explorer to be on whatever browser I now have to use whether it is edge or IE.  I was happy with IE and find it aggravating that years of bookmarks have evaporated.

    michaelbottalico say:

    beerboy1953 say:

    I have the Surface 3 Pro.  I upgraded to Windows 10 and my favorites on Internet Explorer are gone.   Is it possible to get them back somehow?  Also, is it possible to go back to 8.1?   Why does MS make it so difficult when an upgrade happens, it is so frustrating!

    Open Edge. At the right of the bar that has the URL on it , you will see 3 horizontal lines above each other next to a box with a pencil on it. Left click on the 3 lines. You will see a star, some lines, what looks like a clock, and a down arrow. Click on the star and you should see your favorites, If you don't look to the right , under the picture of a pin. Click "import favorites". Once you have that working, go back to the URL bar. At the very right edge are 3 dots " . . . " click there, go to settings at the bottom of that drop down menu. You will see "show the favorites bar" switch, click it to on. Then when you want to add a site just click on the star  on the URL line. Good Luck. This worked for me and others I explained it to.

    Kein Partychat m&#246;glich - zwei Xbox Ones im selben - Microsoft Community

    pin0cci0 say:

    Kein Partychat m&#246;glich - zwei Xbox Ones im selben Netzwerk, FritzBox 7490

    Hallo!

    Leider habe ich große Probleme mit dem Party-Chat von Xbox Live. Wir würden gerne einfach nur zu dritt beim spielen miteinander sprechen können, doch das funktioniert trotz zwei offenen und einem moderaten NAT-Typ leider nicht. Scheinbar ist es dabei auch egal wer die Party hostet. Es läuft immer so ab: Einer hostet die Party, lädt beide ein. Der zweite tritt der Party bei und man kann sich unterhalten. Sobald der dritte jedoch beitritt, kommt erst sehr lange "Verbindung wird hergestellt..." bei der dritten Person, dann steht bei allen dreien "Verbindung wird hergestellt..." und schließlich hat der Dritte die Party wohl übernommen und ist erfolgreich beigetreten, jedoch steht bei den ersten beiden "Verbindung wird hergestellt...". Nach gut einer Minute kommt dann schlussendlich die Meldung, dass ein Netzwerkproblem aufgetreten sei und man es doch bitte noch einmal versuchen solle. Dieses Problem tritt jedoch jedes Mal auf.

    Unsere Konfiguration sieht wie folgt aus:

    Netzwerk 1 - FritzBox 7490 - Änderungen der Sicherheitseinstellungen über UPnP gestatten aktiviert - Teredofilter abgeschaltet - IPv6 abgeschaltet

    --> Xbox 1 als Exposed Host mit offenem NAT-Typ

    --> Xbox 2 über automatische UPnP Freigaben mit moderatem NAT-Typ

     

    Netzwerk 2 - FritzBox FON WLAN 7112 - Änderungen der Sicherheitseinstellungen über UPnP gestatten aktiviert - Teredofilter abgeschaltet - kein IPv6 verfügbar

    --> Xbox 3 als Exposed Host mit offenem NAT-Typ

     

    Meine Fragen sind nun:

    1. Wie ist es möglich beide Xbox Ones in Netzwerk 1 mit offenem NAT-Typ zu betreiben? (ohne Exposed-Host sind leider beide Xbox Ones nur NAT-Typ "moderat")

    2. Wieso ist mit zwei Xbox Ones mit offenem NAT-Typ und einem moderaten NAT-Typ kein Party-Chat möglich? Gibt es noch weitere Einstellungsmöglichkeiten? Das gemeinsame Spielen auf einem offenen Host ist nämlich problemlos möglich, nur das kommunizieren über den Party-Chat leider eben nicht.

    Vielen Dank!

    0 people found this helpful

    Windows Update Agent fails to detect all updates (WSUS with SCCM)

    Howdy

    So we have recently integreated WSUS into SCCM 2012, meaning that WSUS updates are now provided through Software Centre instead of through the Windows Update client. This is working as expected.

    However, we are utilising Kaspersky Endpoint Security, which has a Software Vulnerability Report function that we are keen to use. This would notify us of any machines that fail to have all their updates installed. This is a simpler interface than using SCCM Reporting. When searching for vulnerabilities, Kaspersky's network agent uses the Windows Update Agent service to check into WSUS for updates. This function isn't working correctly on our clients, as it manages to detect ONE single Windows Update. I have an example transcript taken from the WindowsUpdate.log file below:

    As you can see from this transcript only 1 update was found. This was taken from a test machine that was recently built and was missing a large chunk of updates.

    We also have in our infrastructure devices running traditional WSUS on a different server (without SCCM), which are reporting in fine and Kaspersky detects missing updates correctly.

    We have determined with Kaspersky that the issue lies with the Windows Update agent and not their software. Can anyone advise if the issue is because we are using SCCM for updates (and so the Windows Update agent doesn't perform correctly) or that there is another issue that can be resolved?

    Windows 7 Installation failure, Error code: 0x80070017 - Microsoft Community

    cpham111 say:

    Windows 7 Installation failure, Error code: 0x80070017

    I own a legal DVD copy of Windows 7 64 bit. I am attempting to reinstall it on my computer, which at the moment has no operating system installed, but at 13% of expanding windows files, I always get the following error message:

    Windows cannot install the required files. The file may be corrupt or missing. Make sure all files required for installation are available, and restart the installation. Error code: 0x80070017

    What is wrong, how do I fix this? Is my Windows 7 disk damaged?

    trekdozer say:

    If you downloaded Windows 7 and burned it to a DVD try burning it again at the slowest speed possible. It's also possible the download may have errors, you could try downloading it again.

    If you have multiple hard drives remove all except the one you're installing Windows 7 on, then replace after Windows 7 is installed.

    Disconnect all external devices except keyboard and mouse before installing.

    If using a video card and the computer has integrated video use that and remove the video card.

    Unplug your computer from the internet, if you have wireless disable it.

    RAM (memory) - reduce the amount of RAM. 1GB if installing 32bit, 2GB for 64bit, then replace RAM if the upgrade is successful. Also if you just added new RAM make sure it's compatible.

     

     

    Windows 7 Install Disk Not Working

    Just some troubleshooting steps to see if the disk is bad or if the DVD drive is bad:

    If you have another DVD drive available try using that drive in your computer instead.

    If you have another computer available try the Windows 7 disk using that computer and see if it can read the disk, or if the disk can't be read and is bad.

    Also, if you bought the retail version of Windows 7 try putting in the other bit type disk of Windows 7 disk and see if that works properly.

    If you can't boot from the Windows 7 install disk, can your computer boot from other bootable disks?

    How do I use the keyboard on the laptop and not the screen? - Microsoft Community

    jay holmes say:

    How do I use the keyboard on the laptop and not the screen?

    how do I use the keyboard on the laptop instead of having to use the touch screen??

    thanks!!

    basith m say:

    Hi Jay,

    You may use the keyboard after disabling touch and pen feature. I would suggest you to try the following steps to disable touch and pen feature on your computer.

    a. Press Windows + X keys and click on Device Manager.

    b. Select Human Interface Devices.

    c. Search for the Touchscreen drivers.

    d. Right click the Touchscreen and select disable.

    e. Restart the computer and check.

    For further reference, you may refer to the following Microsoft Help article.

    http://windows.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/search-touch-mouse-help#touch-mouse-search-help=windows-8&v1h=win8tab3&v3h=winvistatab1

    Please reply with the status of the issue so that we can confirm that the information is helpful.

    Software won't uninstall in Windows 7 - Microsoft Community

    1hf1 say:

    Software won't uninstall in Windows 7

    I cannot uninstall a backup programme I used  before upgrading to Windows 7. The programme tries to start every time I start up, and I can't uninstall it. The error message says that the prog (Memeo Autobackup) only works with Windows XP or 2000 SP6 (even though it worked with Vista)
    cari [former ms-mvp] say: Start,  (click Orb) and in the box, (type)  msconfig (enter).  Click on the Startup tab.  Do you see the entry for Memeo?  If so uncheck its box.  Click on Apply, OK, then Exit without Restart.

    If there is no entry for Memeo, Start (click Orb), select All Programs and look for the Startup folder.  Is it in there?  If so, highlight, right click and select Delete.

    If neither of those apply, Start, Control Panel, Admin Tools, Services and it should be one of the Services.  Once you find it, set it to Disable.

    Restart the PC.  Have we gotten rid of it?

    windows,
    windows_7,
